msg:It was my first time to visit Yixing. I had to choose between Hilton Garden Inn and Rongda, and finally chose Rongda International. I was not disappointed. It was really comfortable in all aspects. The eye mask and foot mask provided when checking in were so considerate. There were also welcome fruits for check-in. The front desk lady also upgraded the 23F suite floor for free. And a mini teapot was given when checking out. This was so cute. I like it. Thank you for the hotel's careful attention to these small details. â¤ï¸â¤ï¸â¤ï¸

The breakfast in the morning was in the 25F revolving restaurant. There were already many people at 8 o'clock. The seats were by the window. They rotated slowly, and the scenery outside the window was unobstructed. It would be more perfect if there was sunshine. There were many varieties of breakfast, especially the small cakes. There were many varieties, and they were all delicious. Especially the strawberry mousse was delicious. I ate one at a time. I felt that I only came to eat dessert for breakfast.

All rooms have Xiaodu intelligent voice control, which is very convenient. The only regret is that there is no robot ğŸ¤– meal delivery service.

Hygiene: The bathroom is separated into wet and dry areas, with both shower and bathtub. The toilet is a separate cubicle, and the door feels claustrophobic. If you don't mind, it's better to leave the door open.

I came to Yixing for two days during the Qingming Festival. Although I only stayed for one night, I still like it here. It is convenient to travel. There is a park downstairs. The environment is really great. I hope I can stay here again next time.

msg:Great hotel to stay! According to local residents, this is the best hotel in Yixing. Clean, well-kept room. The view from the room is of the city. A deposit of RMB 300 is required upon check-in. It should be noted that the tables are located on a rotating platform, which constantly rotates relative to the axis of the building and the view from the window changes. People with a weak vestibular system may feel uncomfortable. The cuisine is Chinese, but Europeans can definitely find something to eat for breakfast.
